  <span m='4265540'>a</span> <span m='4265590'>second</span> <span m='4265910'>order</span>
  <span m='4266110'>differential</span> <span m='4266550'>equation,</span> <span m='4266950'>like</span>
  <span m='4267190'>we're</span> <span m='4267750'>very</span> <span m='4268010'>much</span>
